Backend Developer)\n\n| Route Path                    | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File             | Context Variables                                                                                                 |\n|-------------------------------|------------------------|----------------|---------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|\n| /                             | root_redirect           | GET            | N/A (redirect)             | None                                                                                                             |\n| /dashboard                    | dashboard              | GET            | dashboard.html            | featured_songs: List[Dict] with keys {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, duration:int}\n  trending_artists: List[Dict] with keys {artist_id:int, name:str, genre:str}                                      |\n| /songs                       | song_catalog           | GET            | song_catalog.html         | songs: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, album_name:str, genre:str, duration:int}\n  genres: List[str] for genre filter options                                                                     |\n| /songs/<int:song_id>         | song_details           | GET            | song_details.html         | song: Dict with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_id:int, artist_name:str, album_id:int, album_name:str, genre:str, duration:int, release_date:str}\n                                         |\n| /playlists                   | my_playlists           | GET            | playlists.html            | playlists: List[Dict] with {playlist_id:int, title:str, description:str, total_songs:int}                                                         |\n| /playlists/<int:playlist_id> | playlist_details       | GET            | playlist_details.html     | playlist: Dict with {playlist_id:int, title:str, description:str}\n  songs_in_playlist: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, duration:int}                                  |\n| /playlists/create            | create_playlist        | GET            | create_playlist.html      | None                                                                                                             |\n| /playlists/create            | save_playlist          | POST           | N/A (redirect or render)  | Form data: playlist_name:str, playlist_description:str                                                             |\n| /albums                     | albums_browse          | GET            | albums.html               | albums: List[Dict] with {album_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, year:int}\n  sort_options: List[str] = [\"By Title\", \"By Artist\", \"By Year\"]                                                    |\n| /albums/<int:album_id>       | album_details          | GET            | album_details.html        | album: Dict with {album_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, year:int}\n  album_songs: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, duration:int}                                 |\n| /artists                    | artist_profiles        | GET            | artists.html              | artists: List[Dict] with {artist_id:int, name:str, genre:str, country:str}\n  sort_options: List[str] = [\"By Name\", \"By Genre\"]                                                      |\n| /artists/<int:artist_id>     | artist_profile         | GET            | artist_profile.html       | artist: Dict with {artist_id:int, name:str, genre:str, country:str, formation_year:int}\n  songs_by_artist: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, album_name:str, duration:int}                         |\n| /genres                     | genre_exploration      | GET            | genres.html               | genres: List[Dict] with {genre_id:int, genre_name:str, description:str}\n  selected_genre: Optional[str]\n  genre_songs: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, duration:int}\n  genre_artists: List[Dict] with {artist_id:int, name:str, genre:str}                                                 |\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)\n\n1. **dashboard.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/dashboard.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Music Streaming Dashboard</title>\n  - <h1>Music Streaming Dashboard</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: dashboard-page\n  - Div: featured-songs\n  - Button: browse-songs-button\n  - Button: my-playlists-button\n  - Button: trending-artists-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - featured_songs: List of dictionaries with keys {song_id, title, artist_name, duration (int seconds)}\n  - trending_artists: List of dictionaries with keys {artist_id, name, genre}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Button ID browse-songs-button -> Flask route function: song_catalog\n  - Button ID my-playlists-button -> Flask route function: my_playlists\n  - Button ID trending-artists-button -> Flask route function: artist_profiles\n\n2. **song_catalog.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/song_catalog.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Song Catalog</title>\n  - <h1>Song Catalog</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: catalog-page\n  - Input: search-input\n  - Dropdown: genre-filter\n  - Div: songs-grid\n  - Button: add-to-playlist-button-{song_id} (dynamic button per song)\n- Context Variables:\n  - songs: List of dicts with {song_id, title, artist_name, album_name, genre, duration}\n  - genres: List of strings (genre names)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - For each add-to-playlist-button-{song_id}, trigger an action to add the song (backend POST or JS)\n\n3. **song_details.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/song_details.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Song Details</title>\n  - <h1 id=\"song-title\">{{ song.title }}</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: song-details-page\n  - H1: song-title\n  - Div: artist-name (artist name is a link to artist_profile route with artist_id)\n  - Div: album-name\n  - Div: duration-display\n  - Button: play-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - song: Dict with keys {song_id, title, artist_id, artist_name, album_id, album_name, genre, duration, release_date}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - artist-name div contains link to artist_profile function with artist_id\n  - play-button triggers song play functionality\n\n4. **playlists.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/playlists.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>My Playlists</title>\n  - <h1>My Playlists</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: playlists-page\n  - Div: playlists-grid\n  - Button: create-playlist-button\n  - Button: view-playlist-button-{playlist_id} (dynamic per playlist)\n  - Button: back-to-dashboard\n- Context Variables:\n  - playlists: List of dicts with {playlist_id, title, description, total_songs}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - create-playlist-button -> create_playlist\n  - view-playlist-button-{playlist_id} -> playlist_details\n  - back-to-dashboard -> dashboard\n\n5. **playlist_details.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/playlist_details.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Playlist Details</title>\n  - <h1 id=\"playlist-title\">{{ playlist.title }}</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: playlist-details-page\n  - H1: playlist-title\n  - Div: playlist-description\n  - Table: songs-in-playlist\n  - Button: remove-song-button-{song_id} (dynamic per song)\n  - Button: delete-playlist-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - playlist: Dict with {playlist_id, title, description}\n  - songs_in_playlist: List of dicts with {song_id, title, artist_name, duration}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - remove-song-button-{song_id} triggers removal of song from playlist\n  - delete-playlist-button triggers playlist deletion\n\n6. **create_playlist.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/create_playlist.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Create New Playlist</title>\n  - <h1>Create New Playlist</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: create-playlist-page\n  - Input: playlist-name-input\n  - Textarea: playlist-description-input\n  - Button: save-playlist-button\n  - Button: cancel-create-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - None (empty form)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - save-playlist-button triggers form submission POST to save_playlist\n  - cancel-create-button redirects back to my_playlists\n\n7. **albums.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/albums.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Albums</title>\n  - <h1>Albums</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: albums-page\n  - Div: albums-grid\n  - Input: search-albums\n  - Dropdown: sort-albums\n  - Button: view-album-button-{album_id} (dynamic per album)\n- Context Variables:\n  - albums: List of dicts with {album_id, title, artist_name, year}\n  - sort_options: List[str] = [\"By Title\", \"By Artist\", \"By Year\"]\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - view-album-button-{album_id} -> album_details\n\n8. **album_details.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/album_details.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Album Details</title>\n  - <h1 id=\"album-title\">{{ album.title }}</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: album-details-page\n  - H1: album-title\n  - Div: album-artist\n  - Div: album-year\n  - Div: album-songs-list\n  - Button: add-album-to-playlist-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - album: Dict with {album_id, title, artist_name, year}\n  - album_songs: List of dicts with {song_id, title, artist_name, duration}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - add-album-to-playlist-button triggers adding all songs to playlist\n\n9. **artists.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/artists.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Artist Profiles</title>\n  - <h1>Artist Profiles</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: artists-page\n  - Div: artists-grid\n  - Input: search-artists\n  - Dropdown: artists-sort\n  - Button: view-artist-button-{artist_id} (dynamic per artist)\n- Context Variables:\n  - artists: List of dicts with {artist_id, name, genre, country}\n  - sort_options: List[str] = [\"By Name\", \"By Genre\"]\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - view-artist-button-{artist_id} -> artist_profile\n\n10. **genres.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/genres.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Genre Exploration</title>\n  - <h1>Genre Exploration</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: genres-page\n  - Div: genres-list\n  - Dropdown: select-genre\n  - Div: genre-songs\n  - Div: genre-artists\n  - Button: back-to-dashboard\n- Context Variables:\n  - genres: List of dicts with {genre_id, genre_name, description}\n  - selected_genre: Optional[str] if any genre selected\n  - genre_songs: List of dicts with {song_id, title, artist_name, duration}\n  - genre_artists: List of dicts with {artist_id, name, genre}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - back-to-dashboard -> dashboard\n  - select-genre dropdown triggers page reload or ajax filtered by genre\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)\n\n1. **data/songs.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. song_id (int): Unique identifier for each song\n  2. title (str): Song title\n  3. artist_id (int): Foreign key referencing artists.txt artist_id\n  4. album_id (int): Foreign key referencing albums.txt album_id\n  5. genre (str): Genre name\n  6. duration (int): Duration of the song in seconds\n  7. release_date (str): Song release date in YYYY-MM-DD format\n  8. play_count (int): Number of times the song has been played\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n```\n\n2. **data/artists.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. artist_id (int): Unique identifier for each artist\n  2. name (str): Artist name\n  3. genre (str): Music genre\n  4. country (str): Country of origin\n  5. formation_year (int): Year the artist or band was formed\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n```\n\n3. **data/albums.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. album_id (int): Unique identifier for each album\n  2. title (str): Album title\n  3. artist_id (int): Foreign key referencing artists.txt artist_id\n  4. release_year (int): Year album was released\n  5. total_songs (int): Number of songs in the album\n  6. genre (str): Album genre\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n```\n\n4. **data/genres.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. genre_id (int): Unique identifier for each genre\n  2. genre_name (str): Name of genre\n  3. description (str): Description of the genre\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n```\n\n5. **data/playlists.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. playlist_id (int): Unique identifier for each playlist\n  2. title (str): Playlist title\n  3. description (str): Playlist description\n  4. creation_date (str): Date playlist was created in YYYY-MM-DD format\n  5. total_songs (int): Number of songs in the playlist\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n```\n\n6. **data/playlist_songs.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. playlist_song_id (int): Unique identifier for each entry\n  2. playlist_id (int): Foreign key referencing playlists.txt playlist_id\n  3. song_id (int): Foreign key referencing songs.txt song_id\n  4. added_date (str): Date song was added to playlist in YYYY-MM-DD format\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|1|2|2025-01-15\n2|1|3|2025-01-15\n3|2|1|2025-01-16\n```\n\n---\n\n*End of MusicStreaming Design Specification.*\n\n\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'MusicStreaming' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'MusicStreaming' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search for songs, create and manage playlists, browse albums, explore artist profiles, filter by genres, and view song/artist statistics. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'MusicStreaming' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' web application will consist of the following ten pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Music Streaming Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured songs, trending artists, and quick navigation to all functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: featured-songs** - Type: Div - Display of featured song recommendations.\n  - **ID: browse-songs-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to song catalog page.\n  - **ID: my-playlists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my playlists page.\n  - **ID: trending-artists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to trending artists page.\n\n### 2. Song Catalog Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Catalog\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available songs with search and filter capabilities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.\n  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search songs by title, artist, or album.\n  - **ID: genre-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by genre (Pop, Rock, Hip-Hop, Jazz, Classical, etc.).\n  - **ID: songs-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying song cards with cover art, title, artist, and duration.\n  - **ID: add-to-playlist-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add song to playlist (each song card has this).\n\n### 3. Song Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific song.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: song-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the song details page.\n  - **ID: song-title** - Type: H1 - Display song title.\n  - **ID: artist-name** - Type: Div - Display artist name with link to artist profile.\n  - **ID: album-name** - Type: Div - Display album name.\n  - **ID: duration-display** - Type: Div - Display song duration.\n  - **ID: play-button** - Type: Button - Button to play the song.\n\n### 4. Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: My Playlists\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all user-created playlists.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlists page.\n  - **ID: playlists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying playlist cards with cover, title, and song count.\n  - **ID: create-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to create a new playlist.\n  - **ID: view-playlist-button-{playlist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view playlist details (each playlist has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 5. Playlist Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Playlist Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying songs in a specific playlist with management options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlist-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlist details page.\n  - **ID: playlist-title** - Type: H1 - Display playlist title.\n  - **ID: playlist-description** - Type: Div - Display playlist description.\n  - **ID: songs-in-playlist** - Type: Table - Table displaying songs with title, artist, duration, and remove option.\n  - **ID: remove-song-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove song from playlist (each song has this).\n  - **ID: delete-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to delete the entire playlist.\n\n### 6. Create Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Create New Playlist\n- **Overview**: A page for users to create a new playlist with title and description.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: create-playlist-page** - Type: Div - Container for the create playlist page.\n  - **ID: playlist-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input playlist name.\n  - **ID: playlist-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input playlist description.\n  - **ID: save-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to save and create the new playlist.\n  - **ID: cancel-create-button** - Type: Button - Button to cancel and go back.\n\n### 7. Album Browse Page\n- **Page Title**: Albums\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available albums with browsing and filtering options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: albums-page** - Type: Div - Container for the albums page.\n  - **ID: albums-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying album cards with cover art, title, artist, and year.\n  - **ID: search-albums** - Type: Input - Field to search albums by title or artist.\n  - **ID: sort-albums** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort albums (By Title, By Artist, By Year).\n  - **ID: view-album-button-{album_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view album details (each album has this).\n\n### 8. Album Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Album Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all songs in a specific album.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: album-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the album details page.\n  - **ID: album-title** - Type: H1 - Display album title.\n  - **ID: album-artist** - Type: Div - Display album artist.\n  - **ID: album-year** - Type: Div - Display album release year.\n  - **ID: album-songs-list** - Type: Div - List of songs in the album.\n  - **ID: add-album-to-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to add all songs from album to playlist.\n\n### 9. Artist Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: Artist Profiles\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all artists and their information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: artists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the artists page.\n  - **ID: artists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying artist cards with photo, name, and genre.\n  - **ID: search-artists** - Type: Input - Field to search artists by name.\n  - **ID: artists-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort artists (By Name, By Genre).\n  - **ID: view-artist-button-{artist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view artist profile (each artist has this).\n\n### 10. Genre Exploration Page\n- **Page Title**: Genre Exploration\n- **Overview**: A page for exploring music by genres with featured songs and artists per genre.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: genres-page** - Type: Div - Container for the genres page.\n  - **ID: genres-list** - Type: Div - List of all available genres.\n  - **ID: select-genre** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select and view a specific genre.\n  - **ID: genre-songs** - Type: Div - Display songs for selected genre.\n  - **ID: genre-artists** - Type: Div - Display artists for selected genre.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  song_id|title|artist_id|album_id|genre|duration|release_date|play_count\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n  2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n  3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n  ```\n\n### 2. Artists Data\n- **File Name**: `artists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  artist_id|name|genre|country|formation_year\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n  2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n  3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n  ```\n\n### 3. Albums Data\n- **File Name**: `albums.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  album_id|title|artist_id|release_year|total_songs|genre\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n  2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n  3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n  ```\n\n### 4. Genres Data\n- **File Name**: `genres.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  genre_id|genre_name|description\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n  2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n  3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n  ```\n\n### 5. Playlists Data\n- **File Name**: `playlists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_id|title|description|creation_date|total_songs\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n  2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n  3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n  ```\n\n### 6. Playlist Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `playlist_songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_song_id|playlist_id|song_id|added_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|1|3|2025-01-15\n  3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n",

0)\n    sorted_artists = sorted(artists, key=lambda a: artist_play_counts.get(a['artist_id'], 0), reverse=True)\n    trending_artists = []\n    for artist in sorted_artists[:5]:\n        trending_artists.append({\n            'artist_id': artist['artist_id'],\n            'name': artist['name'],\n            'genre': artist['genre']\n        })\n\n    return select-genre dropdown triggers page reload or ajax filtered by genre\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)\n\n1. **data/songs.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. song_id (int): Unique identifier for each song\n  2. title (str): Song title\n  3. artist_id (int): Foreign key referencing artists.txt artist_id\n  4. album_id (int): Foreign key referencing albums.txt album_id\n  5. genre (str): Genre name\n  6. duration (int): Duration of the song in seconds\n  7. release_date (str): Song release date in YYYY-MM-DD format\n  8. play_count (int): Number of times the song has been played\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n```\n\n2. **data/artists.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. artist_id (int): Unique identifier for each artist\n  2. name (str): Artist name\n  3. genre (str): Music genre\n  4. country (str): Country of origin\n  5. formation_year (int): Year the artist or band was formed\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n```\n\n3. **data/albums.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. album_id (int): Unique identifier for each album\n  2. title (str): Album title\n  3. artist_id (int): Foreign key referencing artists.txt artist_id\n  4. release_year (int): Year album was released\n  5. total_songs (int): Number of songs in the album\n  6. genre (str): Album genre\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n```\n\n4. **data/genres.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. genre_id (int): Unique identifier for each genre\n  2. genre_name (str): Name of genre\n  3. description (str): Description of the genre\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n```\n\n5. **data/playlists.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. playlist_id (int): Unique identifier for each playlist\n  2. title (str): Playlist title\n  3. description (str): Playlist description\n  4. creation_date (str): Date playlist was created in YYYY-MM-DD format\n  5. total_songs (int): Number of songs in the playlist\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n```\n\n6. **data/playlist_songs.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. playlist_song_id (int): Unique identifier for each entry\n  2. playlist_id (int): Foreign key referencing playlists.txt playlist_id\n  3. song_id (int): Foreign key referencing songs.txt song_id\n  4. added_date (str): Date song was added to playlist in YYYY-MM-DD format\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|1|2|2025-01-15\n2|1|3|2025-01-15\n3|2|1|2025-01-16\n```\n\n---\n\n*End of MusicStreaming Design Specification.*\n\n\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'MusicStreaming' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'MusicStreaming' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search for songs, create and manage playlists, browse albums, explore artist profiles, filter by genres, and view song/artist statistics. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'MusicStreaming' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' web application will consist of the following ten pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Music Streaming Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured songs, trending artists, and quick navigation to all functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: featured-songs** - Type: Div - Display of featured song recommendations.\n  - **ID: browse-songs-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to song catalog page.\n  - **ID: my-playlists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my playlists page.\n  - **ID: trending-artists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to trending artists page.\n\n### 2. Song Catalog Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Catalog\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available songs with search and filter capabilities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.\n  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search songs by title, artist, or album.\n  - **ID: genre-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by genre (Pop, Rock, Hip-Hop, Jazz, Classical, etc.).\n  - **ID: songs-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying song cards with cover art, title, artist, and duration.\n  - **ID: add-to-playlist-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add song to playlist (each song card has this).\n\n### 3. Song Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific song.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: song-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the song details page.\n  - **ID: song-title** - Type: H1 - Display song title.\n  - **ID: artist-name** - Type: Div - Display artist name with link to artist profile.\n  - **ID: album-name** - Type: Div - Display album name.\n  - **ID: duration-display** - Type: Div - Display song duration.\n  - **ID: play-button** - Type: Button - Button to play the song.\n\n### 4. Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: My Playlists\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all user-created playlists.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlists page.\n  - **ID: playlists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying playlist cards with cover, title, and song count.\n  - **ID: create-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to create a new playlist.\n  - **ID: view-playlist-button-{playlist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view playlist details (each playlist has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 5. Playlist Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Playlist Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying songs in a specific playlist with management options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlist-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlist details page.\n  - **ID: playlist-title** - Type: H1 - Display playlist title.\n  - **ID: playlist-description** - Type: Div - Display playlist description.\n  - **ID: songs-in-playlist** - Type: Table - Table displaying songs with title, artist, duration, and remove option.\n  - **ID: remove-song-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove song from playlist (each song has this).\n  - **ID: delete-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to delete the entire playlist.\n\n### 6. Create Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Create New Playlist\n- **Overview**: A page for users to create a new playlist with title and description.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: create-playlist-page** - Type: Div - Container for the create playlist page.\n  - **ID: playlist-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input playlist name.\n  - **ID: playlist-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input playlist description.\n  - **ID: save-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to save and create the new playlist.\n  - **ID: cancel-create-button** - Type: Button - Button to cancel and go back.\n\n### 7. Album Browse Page\n- **Page Title**: Albums\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available albums with browsing and filtering options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: albums-page** - Type: Div - Container for the albums page.\n  - **ID: albums-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying album cards with cover art, title, artist, and year.\n  - **ID: search-albums** - Type: Input - Field to search albums by title or artist.\n  - **ID: sort-albums** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort albums (By Title, By Artist, By Year).\n  - **ID: view-album-button-{album_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view album details (each album has this).\n\n### 8. Album Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Album Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all songs in a specific album.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: album-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the album details page.\n  - **ID: album-title** - Type: H1 - Display album title.\n  - **ID: album-artist** - Type: Div - Display album artist.\n  - **ID: album-year** - Type: Div - Display album release year.\n  - **ID: album-songs-list** - Type: Div - List of songs in the album.\n  - **ID: add-album-to-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to add all songs from album to playlist.\n\n### 9. Artist Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: Artist Profiles\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all artists and their information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: artists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the artists page.\n  - **ID: artists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying artist cards with photo, name, and genre.\n  - **ID: search-artists** - Type: Input - Field to search artists by name.\n  - **ID: artists-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort artists (By Name, By Genre).\n  - **ID: view-artist-button-{artist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view artist profile (each artist has this).\n\n### 10. Genre Exploration Page\n- **Page Title**: Genre Exploration\n- **Overview**: A page for exploring music by genres with featured songs and artists per genre.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: genres-page** - Type: Div - Container for the genres page.\n  - **ID: genres-list** - Type: Div - List of all available genres.\n  - **ID: select-genre** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select and view a specific genre.\n  - **ID: genre-songs** - Type: Div - Display songs for selected genre.\n  - **ID: genre-artists** - Type: Div - Display artists for selected genre.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  song_id|title|artist_id|album_id|genre|duration|release_date|play_count\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n  2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n  3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n  ```\n\n### 2. Artists Data\n- **File Name**: `artists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  artist_id|name|genre|country|formation_year\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n  2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n  3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n  ```\n\n### 3. Albums Data\n- **File Name**: `albums.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  album_id|title|artist_id|release_year|total_songs|genre\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n  2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n  3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n  ```\n\n### 4. Genres Data\n- **File Name**: `genres.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  genre_id|genre_name|description\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n  2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n  3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n  ```\n\n### 5. Playlists Data\n- **File Name**: `playlists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_id|title|description|creation_date|total_songs\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n  2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n  3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n  ```\n\n### 6. Playlist Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `playlist_songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_song_id|playlist_id|song_id|added_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|1|3|2025-01-15\n  3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n",

Backend Developer)\n\n| Route Path                    | Function Name           | HTTP Method(s) | Template File             | Context Variables                                                                                                 |\n|-------------------------------|------------------------|----------------|---------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|\n| /                             | root_redirect           | GET            | N/A (redirect)             | None                                                                                                             |\n| /dashboard                    | dashboard              | GET            | dashboard.html            | featured_songs: List[Dict] with keys {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, duration:int}\n  trending_artists: List[Dict] with keys {artist_id:int, name:str, genre:str}                                      |\n| /songs                       | song_catalog           | GET            | song_catalog.html         | songs: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, album_name:str, genre:str, duration:int}\n  genres: List[str] for genre filter options                                                                     |\n| /songs/<int:song_id>         | song_details           | GET            | song_details.html         | song: Dict with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_id:int, artist_name:str, album_id:int, album_name:str, genre:str, duration:int, release_date:str}\n                                         |\n| /playlists                   | my_playlists           | GET            | playlists.html            | playlists: List[Dict] with {playlist_id:int, title:str, description:str, total_songs:int}                                                         |\n| /playlists/<int:playlist_id> | playlist_details       | GET            | playlist_details.html     | playlist: Dict with {playlist_id:int, title:str, description:str}\n  songs_in_playlist: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, duration:int}                                  |\n| /playlists/create            | create_playlist        | GET            | create_playlist.html      | None                                                                                                             |\n| /playlists/create            | save_playlist          | POST           | N/A (redirect or render)  | Form data: playlist_name:str, playlist_description:str                                                             |\n| /albums                     | albums_browse          | GET            | albums.html               | albums: List[Dict] with {album_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, year:int}\n  sort_options: List[str] = [\"By Title\", \"By Artist\", \"By Year\"]                                                    |\n| /albums/<int:album_id>       | album_details          | GET            | album_details.html        | album: Dict with {album_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, year:int}\n  album_songs: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, duration:int}                                 |\n| /artists                    | artist_profiles        | GET            | artists.html              | artists: List[Dict] with {artist_id:int, name:str, genre:str, country:str}\n  sort_options: List[str] = [\"By Name\", \"By Genre\"]                                                      |\n| /artists/<int:artist_id>     | artist_profile         | GET            | artist_profile.html       | artist: Dict with {artist_id:int, name:str, genre:str, country:str, formation_year:int}\n  songs_by_artist: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, album_name:str, duration:int}                         |\n| /genres                     | genre_exploration      | GET            | genres.html               | genres: List[Dict] with {genre_id:int, genre_name:str, description:str}\n  selected_genre: Optional[str]\n  genre_songs: List[Dict] with {song_id:int, title:str, artist_name:str, duration:int}\n  genre_artists: List[Dict] with {artist_id:int, name:str, genre:str}                                                 |\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)\n\n1. **dashboard.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/dashboard.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Music Streaming Dashboard</title>\n  - <h1>Music Streaming Dashboard</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: dashboard-page\n  - Div: featured-songs\n  - Button: browse-songs-button\n  - Button: my-playlists-button\n  - Button: trending-artists-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - featured_songs: List of dictionaries with keys {song_id, title, artist_name, duration (int seconds)}\n  - trending_artists: List of dictionaries with keys {artist_id, name, genre}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Button ID browse-songs-button -> Flask route function: song_catalog\n  - Button ID my-playlists-button -> Flask route function: my_playlists\n  - Button ID trending-artists-button -> Flask route function: artist_profiles\n\n2. **song_catalog.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/song_catalog.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Song Catalog</title>\n  - <h1>Song Catalog</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: catalog-page\n  - Input: search-input\n  - Dropdown: genre-filter\n  - Div: songs-grid\n  - Button: add-to-playlist-button-{song_id} (dynamic button per song)\n- Context Variables:\n  - songs: List of dicts with {song_id, title, artist_name, album_name, genre, duration}\n  - genres: List of strings (genre names)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - For each add-to-playlist-button-{song_id}, trigger an action to add the song (backend POST or JS)\n\n3. **song_details.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/song_details.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Song Details</title>\n  - <h1 id=\"song-title\">{{ song.title }}</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: song-details-page\n  - H1: song-title\n  - Div: artist-name (artist name is a link to artist_profile route with artist_id)\n  - Div: album-name\n  - Div: duration-display\n  - Button: play-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - song: Dict with keys {song_id, title, artist_id, artist_name, album_id, album_name, genre, duration, release_date}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - artist-name div contains link to artist_profile function with artist_id\n  - play-button triggers song play functionality\n\n4. **playlists.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/playlists.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>My Playlists</title>\n  - <h1>My Playlists</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: playlists-page\n  - Div: playlists-grid\n  - Button: create-playlist-button\n  - Button: view-playlist-button-{playlist_id} (dynamic per playlist)\n  - Button: back-to-dashboard\n- Context Variables:\n  - playlists: List of dicts with {playlist_id, title, description, total_songs}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - create-playlist-button -> create_playlist\n  - view-playlist-button-{playlist_id} -> playlist_details\n  - back-to-dashboard -> dashboard\n\n5. **playlist_details.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/playlist_details.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Playlist Details</title>\n  - <h1 id=\"playlist-title\">{{ playlist.title }}</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: playlist-details-page\n  - H1: playlist-title\n  - Div: playlist-description\n  - Table: songs-in-playlist\n  - Button: remove-song-button-{song_id} (dynamic per song)\n  - Button: delete-playlist-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - playlist: Dict with {playlist_id, title, description}\n  - songs_in_playlist: List of dicts with {song_id, title, artist_name, duration}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - remove-song-button-{song_id} triggers removal of song from playlist\n  - delete-playlist-button triggers playlist deletion\n\n6. **create_playlist.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/create_playlist.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Create New Playlist</title>\n  - <h1>Create New Playlist</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: create-playlist-page\n  - Input: playlist-name-input\n  - Textarea: playlist-description-input\n  - Button: save-playlist-button\n  - Button: cancel-create-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - None (empty form)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - save-playlist-button triggers form submission POST to save_playlist\n  - cancel-create-button redirects back to my_playlists\n\n7. **albums.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/albums.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Albums</title>\n  - <h1>Albums</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: albums-page\n  - Div: albums-grid\n  - Input: search-albums\n  - Dropdown: sort-albums\n  - Button: view-album-button-{album_id} (dynamic per album)\n- Context Variables:\n  - albums: List of dicts with {album_id, title, artist_name, year}\n  - sort_options: List[str] = [\"By Title\", \"By Artist\", \"By Year\"]\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - view-album-button-{album_id} -> album_details\n\n8. **album_details.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/album_details.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Album Details</title>\n  - <h1 id=\"album-title\">{{ album.title }}</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: album-details-page\n  - H1: album-title\n  - Div: album-artist\n  - Div: album-year\n  - Div: album-songs-list\n  - Button: add-album-to-playlist-button\n- Context Variables:\n  - album: Dict with {album_id, title, artist_name, year}\n  - album_songs: List of dicts with {song_id, title, artist_name, duration}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - add-album-to-playlist-button triggers adding all songs to playlist\n\n9. **artists.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/artists.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Artist Profiles</title>\n  - <h1>Artist Profiles</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: artists-page\n  - Div: artists-grid\n  - Input: search-artists\n  - Dropdown: artists-sort\n  - Button: view-artist-button-{artist_id} (dynamic per artist)\n- Context Variables:\n  - artists: List of dicts with {artist_id, name, genre, country}\n  - sort_options: List[str] = [\"By Name\", \"By Genre\"]\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - view-artist-button-{artist_id} -> artist_profile\n\n10. **genres.html**\n- Template File Path: templates/genres.html\n- Page Title:\n  - <title>Genre Exploration</title>\n  - <h1>Genre Exploration</h1>\n- Required Element IDs:\n  - Div: genres-page\n  - Div: genres-list\n  - Dropdown: select-genre\n  - Div: genre-songs\n  - Div: genre-artists\n  - Button: back-to-dashboard\n- Context Variables:\n  - genres: List of dicts with {genre_id, genre_name, description}\n  - selected_genre: Optional[str] if any genre selected\n  - genre_songs: List of dicts with {song_id, title, artist_name, duration}\n  - genre_artists: List of dicts with {artist_id, name, genre}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - back-to-dashboard -> dashboard\n  - select-genre dropdown triggers page reload or ajax filtered by genre\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)\n\n1. **data/songs.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. song_id (int): Unique identifier for each song\n  2. title (str): Song title\n  3. artist_id (int): Foreign key referencing artists.txt artist_id\n  4. album_id (int): Foreign key referencing albums.txt album_id\n  5. genre (str): Genre name\n  6. duration (int): Duration of the song in seconds\n  7. release_date (str): Song release date in YYYY-MM-DD format\n  8. play_count (int): Number of times the song has been played\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n```\n\n2. **data/artists.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. artist_id (int): Unique identifier for each artist\n  2. name (str): Artist name\n  3. genre (str): Music genre\n  4. country (str): Country of origin\n  5. formation_year (int): Year the artist or band was formed\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n```\n\n3. **data/albums.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. album_id (int): Unique identifier for each album\n  2. title (str): Album title\n  3. artist_id (int): Foreign key referencing artists.txt artist_id\n  4. release_year (int): Year album was released\n  5. total_songs (int): Number of songs in the album\n  6. genre (str): Album genre\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n```\n\n4. **data/genres.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. genre_id (int): Unique identifier for each genre\n  2. genre_name (str): Name of genre\n  3. description (str): Description of the genre\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n```\n\n5. **data/playlists.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. playlist_id (int): Unique identifier for each playlist\n  2. title (str): Playlist title\n  3. description (str): Playlist description\n  4. creation_date (str): Date playlist was created in YYYY-MM-DD format\n  5. total_songs (int): Number of songs in the playlist\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n```\n\n6. **data/playlist_songs.txt**\n- File format: pipe-delimited (|)\n- Fields:\n  1. playlist_song_id (int): Unique identifier for each entry\n  2. playlist_id (int): Foreign key referencing playlists.txt playlist_id\n  3. song_id (int): Foreign key referencing songs.txt song_id\n  4. added_date (str): Date song was added to playlist in YYYY-MM-DD format\n- Example rows:\n```\n1|1|2|2025-01-15\n2|1|3|2025-01-15\n3|2|1|2025-01-16\n```\n\n---\n\n*End of MusicStreaming Design Specification.*\n\n\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'MusicStreaming' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'MusicStreaming' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search for songs, create and manage playlists, browse albums, explore artist profiles, filter by genres, and view song/artist statistics. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'MusicStreaming' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' web application will consist of the following ten pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Music Streaming Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured songs, trending artists, and quick navigation to all functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: featured-songs** - Type: Div - Display of featured song recommendations.\n  - **ID: browse-songs-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to song catalog page.\n  - **ID: my-playlists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to my playlists page.\n  - **ID: trending-artists-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to trending artists page.\n\n### 2. Song Catalog Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Catalog\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available songs with search and filter capabilities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.\n  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search songs by title, artist, or album.\n  - **ID: genre-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by genre (Pop, Rock, Hip-Hop, Jazz, Classical, etc.).\n  - **ID: songs-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying song cards with cover art, title, artist, and duration.\n  - **ID: add-to-playlist-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add song to playlist (each song card has this).\n\n### 3. Song Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Song Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific song.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: song-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the song details page.\n  - **ID: song-title** - Type: H1 - Display song title.\n  - **ID: artist-name** - Type: Div - Display artist name with link to artist profile.\n  - **ID: album-name** - Type: Div - Display album name.\n  - **ID: duration-display** - Type: Div - Display song duration.\n  - **ID: play-button** - Type: Button - Button to play the song.\n\n### 4. Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: My Playlists\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all user-created playlists.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlists page.\n  - **ID: playlists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying playlist cards with cover, title, and song count.\n  - **ID: create-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to create a new playlist.\n  - **ID: view-playlist-button-{playlist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view playlist details (each playlist has this).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 5. Playlist Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Playlist Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying songs in a specific playlist with management options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: playlist-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the playlist details page.\n  - **ID: playlist-title** - Type: H1 - Display playlist title.\n  - **ID: playlist-description** - Type: Div - Display playlist description.\n  - **ID: songs-in-playlist** - Type: Table - Table displaying songs with title, artist, duration, and remove option.\n  - **ID: remove-song-button-{song_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove song from playlist (each song has this).\n  - **ID: delete-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to delete the entire playlist.\n\n### 6. Create Playlist Page\n- **Page Title**: Create New Playlist\n- **Overview**: A page for users to create a new playlist with title and description.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: create-playlist-page** - Type: Div - Container for the create playlist page.\n  - **ID: playlist-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input playlist name.\n  - **ID: playlist-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input playlist description.\n  - **ID: save-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to save and create the new playlist.\n  - **ID: cancel-create-button** - Type: Button - Button to cancel and go back.\n\n### 7. Album Browse Page\n- **Page Title**: Albums\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available albums with browsing and filtering options.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: albums-page** - Type: Div - Container for the albums page.\n  - **ID: albums-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying album cards with cover art, title, artist, and year.\n  - **ID: search-albums** - Type: Input - Field to search albums by title or artist.\n  - **ID: sort-albums** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort albums (By Title, By Artist, By Year).\n  - **ID: view-album-button-{album_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view album details (each album has this).\n\n### 8. Album Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Album Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all songs in a specific album.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: album-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the album details page.\n  - **ID: album-title** - Type: H1 - Display album title.\n  - **ID: album-artist** - Type: Div - Display album artist.\n  - **ID: album-year** - Type: Div - Display album release year.\n  - **ID: album-songs-list** - Type: Div - List of songs in the album.\n  - **ID: add-album-to-playlist-button** - Type: Button - Button to add all songs from album to playlist.\n\n### 9. Artist Profile Page\n- **Page Title**: Artist Profiles\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all artists and their information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: artists-page** - Type: Div - Container for the artists page.\n  - **ID: artists-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying artist cards with photo, name, and genre.\n  - **ID: search-artists** - Type: Input - Field to search artists by name.\n  - **ID: artists-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort artists (By Name, By Genre).\n  - **ID: view-artist-button-{artist_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view artist profile (each artist has this).\n\n### 10. Genre Exploration Page\n- **Page Title**: Genre Exploration\n- **Overview**: A page for exploring music by genres with featured songs and artists per genre.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: genres-page** - Type: Div - Container for the genres page.\n  - **ID: genres-list** - Type: Div - List of all available genres.\n  - **ID: select-genre** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select and view a specific genre.\n  - **ID: genre-songs** - Type: Div - Display songs for selected genre.\n  - **ID: genre-artists** - Type: Div - Display artists for selected genre.\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'MusicStreaming' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. Songs Data\n- **File Name**: `songs.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  song_id|title|artist_id|album_id|genre|duration|release_date|play_count\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Bohemian Rhapsody|1|1|Rock|354|1975-10-31|2500000\n  2|Blinding Lights|2|2|Synth-Pop|200|2019-11-29|3800000\n  3|Shape of You|3|3|Pop|233|2017-01-06|4200000\n  ```\n\n### 2. Artists Data\n- **File Name**: `artists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  artist_id|name|genre|country|formation_year\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Queen|Rock|United Kingdom|1970\n  2|The Weeknd|Synth-Pop|Canada|2010\n  3|Ed Sheeran|Pop|United Kingdom|2005\n  ```\n\n### 3. Albums Data\n- **File Name**: `albums.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  album_id|title|artist_id|release_year|total_songs|genre\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|A Night at the Opera|1|1975|11|Rock\n  2|After Hours|2|2019|14|Synth-Pop\n  3|Divide|3|2017|12|Pop\n  ```\n\n### 4. Genres Data\n- **File Name**: `genres.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  genre_id|genre_name|description\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Rock|Guitar-driven music with strong beats and vocals\n  2|Pop|Catchy mainstream music with broad appeal\n  3|Hip-Hop|Rhythmic music with rap vocals and beat production\n  ```\n\n### 5. Playlists Data\n- **File Name**: `playlists.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  playlist_id|title|description|creation_date|total_songs\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Workout Mix|High energy songs for the gym|2025-01-15|25\n  2|Chill Vibes|Relaxing music for study|2025-01-16|18\n  3|Party Hits|Latest party tracks|2025-01-17|32\n  ```\n\n### 6.
